  company_name STRING,
  waste_type STRING,
  weight FLOAT
);

CREATE TABLE eco_friendly_products (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  product_name STRING,
  price FLOAT,
  carbon_offset FLOAT
);

CREATE TABLE carbon_footprint (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  company_name STRING,
  emission_level FLOAT
);

CREATE TABLE energy_consumption (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  device_id UUID,
  consumption FLOAT,
  timestamp TIMESTAMP
);</t><s>upsert into energy_consumption (id, device_id, consumption, timestamp) values ('2dbe9cc8-4c8a-4f54-a3d9-e25e7d759ad2', '23aa7f10-0bc4-4cf5-9ec3-43d7a44fb89f', 100.25, '2022-10-05 08:00:00') on conflict (id) do update set device_id = excluded.device_id, consumption = excluded.consumption, timestamp = excluded.timestamp;</s>

CREATE TABLE sustainability_progress (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_id INT, metric_id INT, progress_value FLOAT, date_recorded DATE)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_metrics (id INT PRIMARY KEY, metric_name TEXT, description TEXT, target_value FLOAT, actual_value FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_initiatives (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_name TEXT, description TEXT, start_date DATE, end_date DATE)</t><s>UPSERT INTO environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) VALUES (1, 'Climate Change', 'Description of climate change impact', 'Environmental'), ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name=EXCLUDED.name, description=EXCLUDED.description, impact_type=EXCLUDED.impact_type</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE sustainability_goals (id INT PRIMARY KEY, goal_name TEXT, target TEXT, completion_date DATE)

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_progress (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_id INT, metric_id INT, progress_value FLOAT, date_recorded DATE)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_metrics (id INT PRIMARY KEY, metric_name TEXT, description TEXT, target_value FLOAT, actual_value FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_initiatives (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_name TEXT, description TEXT, start_date DATE, end_date DATE)</t><s>upsert into environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) values (1, 'climate change', 'description of climate change impact', 'environmental'), on conflict (id) do update set name=excluded.name, description=excluded.description, impact_type=excluded.impact_type</s>

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)</t><s>upsert into environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) values (1, 'climate change', 'description of climate change impact', 'environmental'), on conflict (id) do update set name=excluded.name, description=excluded.description, impact_type=excluded.impact_type</s>

CREATE TABLE sustainability_progress (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_id INT, metric_id INT, progress_value FLOAT, date_recorded DATE)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_initiatives (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_name TEXT, description TEXT, start_date DATE, end_date DATE)</t><s>UPSERT INTO environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) VALUES (1, 'Climate Change', 'Description of climate change impact', 'Environmental'), ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name=EXCLUDED.name, description=EXCLUDED.description, impact_type=EXCLUDED.impact_type</s>

CREATE TABLE sustainability_metrics (id INT PRIMARY KEY, metric_name TEXT, description TEXT, target_value FLOAT, actual_value FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_goals (id INT PRIMARY KEY, goal_name TEXT, target TEXT, completion_date DATE)</t><s>upsert into environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) values (1, 'climate change', 'description of climate change impact', 'environmental'), on conflict (id) do update set name=excluded.name, description=excluded.description, impact_type=excluded.impact_type</s>

CREATE TABLE sustainability_goals (id INT PRIMARY KEY, goal_name TEXT, target TEXT, completion_date DATE)

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)</t><s>UPSERT INTO environmental_impact (id, name, description, impact_type) VALUES (1, 'Climate Change', 'Description of climate change impact', 'Environmental'), ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name=EXCLUDED.name, description=EXCLUDED.description, impact_type=EXCLUDED.impact_type</s>

CREATE TABLE sustainability_metrics (id INT PRIMARY KEY, metric_name TEXT, description TEXT, target_value FLOAT, actual_value FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_progress (id INT PRIMARY KEY, initiative_id INT, metric_id INT, progress_value FLOAT, date_recorded DATE)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_goals (id INT PRIMARY KEY, goal_name TEXT, target TEXT, completion_date DATE)</t><s>UPSERT INTO sustainability_goals (id, goal_name, target, completion_date) VALUES (1, 'Reduce Carbon Footprint', '20%', '2025-12-31'), ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET goal_name=EXCLUDED.goal_name, target=EXCLUDED.target, completion_date=EXCLUDED.completion_date</s>

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)</t><s>UPSERT INTO sustainability_initiatives (id, initiative_name, description, start_date, end_date) VALUES (1, 'Green Energy Plan', 'Description of green energy initiative', '2022-01-01', '2025-12-31'), ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET initiative_name=EXCLUDED.initiative_name, description=EXCLUDED.description, start_date=EXCLUDED.start_date, end_date=EXCLUDED.end_date</s>
